    const now = value.clone().month(newMonth);\n                    onChange(now);\n                  }}\n                />\n              </Col>\n              <Col>\n                <Radio.Group\n                  size=\"small\"\n                  onChange={(e) => onTypeChange(e.target.value)}\n                  value={type}\n                >\n                  <Radio.Button value=\"month\">月</Radio.Button>\n                  <Radio.Button value=\"year\">年</Radio.Button>\n                </Radio.Group>\n              </Col>\n            </Row>\n          );\n        }}\n      />\n    </div>\n  );\n};\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Show Week\n\nShow week number in fullscreen calendar by setting `showWeek` prop to `true`.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { Calendar } from 'antd';\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <>\n    <Calendar fullscreen showWeek />\n    <br />\n    <Calendar fullscreen={false} showWeek />\n  </>\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Customize Header\n\nCustomize Calendar header content.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport dayjs from 'dayjs';\n\nimport 'dayjs/locale/zh-cn';\n\nimport { Calendar, Flex, Radio, Select, theme, Typography } from 'antd';\nimport type { CalendarProps } from 'antd';\nimport type { Dayjs } from 'dayjs';\nimport dayLocaleData from 'dayjs/plugin/localeData';\n\ndayjs.extend(dayLocaleData);\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => {\n  const { token } = theme.useToken();\n\n  const onPanelChange = (value: Dayjs, mode: CalendarProps<Dayjs>['mode']) => {\n    console.log(value.format('YYYY-MM-DD'), mode);\n  };\n\n  const wrapperStyle: React.CSSProperties = {\n    width: 300,\n    border: `1px solid ${token.colorBorderSecondary}`,\n    borderRadius: token.borderRadiusLG,\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div style={wrapperStyle}>\n      <Calendar\n        fullscreen={false}\n        headerRender={({ value, type, onChange, onTypeChange }) => {\n          const year = value.year();\n          const month = value.month();\n\n          const yearOptions = Array.from({ length: 20 }, (_, i) => {\n            const label = year - 10 + i;\n            return { label, value: label };\n          });\n\n          const monthOptions = value\n            .localeData()\n            .monthsShort()\n            .map((label, index) => ({\n              label,\n              value: index,\n            }));\n\n          return (\n            <div style={{ padding: 8 }}>\n              <Typography.Title level={4}>Custom header</Typography.Title>\n              <Flex gap={8}>\n                <Radio.Group\n                  size=\"small\"\n                  onChange={(e) => onTypeChange(e.target.value)}\n                  value={type}\n                >\n                  <Radio.Button value=\"month\">Month</Radio.Button>\n                  <Radio.Button value=\"year\">Year</Radio.Button>\n                </Radio.Group>\n                <Select\n                  size=\"small\"\n                  popupMatchSelectWidth={false}\n                  value={year}\n                  options={yearOptions}\n                  onChange={(newYear) => {\n                    const now = value.clone().year(newYear);\n                    onChange(now);\n                  }}\n                />\n                <Select\n                  size=\"small\"\n                  popupMatchSelectWidth={false}\n                  value={month}\n                  options={monthOptions}\n                  onChange={(newMonth) => {\n                    const now = value.clone().month(newMonth);\n                    onChange(now);\n                  }}\n                />\n              </Flex>\n            </div>\n          );\n        }}\n        onPanelChange={onPanelChange}\n      />\n    </div>\n  );\n};\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Custom semantic dom styling\n\nYou can customize the [semantic dom](#semantic-dom) style of Calendar by passing objects/functions through `classNames` and `styles`.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { Calendar, Flex } from 'antd';\nimport type { CalendarProps, GetProp } from 'antd';\nimport { createStyles } from 'antd-style';\nimport type { Dayjs } from 'dayjs';\n\nconst useStyles = createStyles(({ token }) => ({\n  root: {\n    padding: 10,\n    backgroundColor: token.colorPrimaryBg,\n  },\n}));\n\nconst stylesObject: CalendarProps<Dayjs>['styles'] = {\n  root: {\n    borderRadius: 8,\n    width: 600,\n  },\n};\n\nconst stylesFunction: CalendarProps<Dayjs>['styles'] = (\n  info,\n): GetProp<CalendarProps<Dayjs>, 'styles', 'Return'> => {\n  if (info.props.fullscreen) {\n    return {\n      root: {\n        border: '2px solid #BDE3C3',\n        borderRadius: 10,\n        backgroundColor: 'rgba(189,227,195, 0.3)',\n      },\n    };\n  }\n};\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => {\n  const { styles: classNames } = useStyles();\n  return (\n    <Flex vertical gap=\"medium\">\n      <Calendar fullscreen={false} classNames={classNames} styles={stylesObject} />\n      <Calendar classNames={classNames} styles={stylesFunction} />\n    </Flex>\n  );\n};\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n## API\n\nCommon props ref：[Common props](/docs/react/common-props)\n\n**Note:** Part of the Calendar's locale is read from `value`. So, please set the locale of `dayjs` correctly.\n\n```jsx\n// The default locale is en-US, if you want to use other locale, just set locale in entry file globally.\n// import dayjs from 'dayjs';\n// import 'dayjs/locale/zh-cn';\n// dayjs.locale('zh-cn');\n\n<Calendar cellRender={cellRender} onPanelChange={onPanelChange} onSelect={onSelect} />\n```\n\n| Property | Description | Type | Default | Version | [Global Config](/components/config-provider#component-config) |\n| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |\n| cellRender | Customize cell content | function(current: dayjs, info: { prefixCls: string, originNode: React.ReactElement, today: dayjs, range?: 'start' \\| 'end', type: PanelMode, locale?: Locale, subType?: 'hour' \\| 'minute' \\| 'second' \\| 'meridiem' }) => React.ReactNode | - | 5.4.0 | × |\n| classNames | Customize class for each semantic structure inside the component. Supports object or function. | Record<[SemanticDOM](#semantic-dom), string> \\| (info: { props })=> Record<[SemanticDOM](#semantic-dom), string> | - | | 6.0.0 |\n| ~~dateFullCellRender~~ | Customize the display of the date cell, the returned content will override the cell. Please use `fullCellRender` instead in 5.4.0 and later | function(date: Dayjs): ReactNode | - | < 5.4.0 | × |\n| fullCellRender | Customize cell content | function(current: dayjs, info: { prefixCls: string, originNode: React.ReactElement, today: dayjs, range?: 'start' \\| 'end', type: PanelMode, locale?: Locale, subType?: 'hour' \\| 'minute' \\| 'second' \\| 'meridiem' }) => React.ReactNode | - | 5.4.0 | × |\n| defaultValue | The date selected by default | [dayjs](https://day.js.org/) | - | | × |\n| disabledDate | Function that specifies the dates that cannot be selected, `currentDate` is same dayjs object as `value` prop which you shouldn't mutate it (https://github.com/ant-design/ant-design/issues/30987) | (currentDate: Dayjs) => boolean | - | | × |\n| fullscreen | Whether to display in full-screen | boolean | true | | × |\n| showWeek | Whether to display week number | boolean | false | 5.23.0 | × |\n| styles | Customize inline style for each semantic structure inside the component. Supports object or function. | Record<[SemanticDOM](#semantic-dom), CSSProperties> \\| (info: { props })=> Record<[SemanticDOM](#semantic-dom), CSSProperties> | - | | 6.0.0 |\n| headerRender | Render custom header in panel | function(object:{value: Dayjs, type: 'year' \\| 'month', onChange: f(), onTypeChange: f()}) | - | | × |\n| locale | The calendar's locale | object | [(default)](https://github.com/ant-design/ant-design/blob/master/components/date-picker/locale/example.json) | | × |\n| mode | The display mode of the calendar | `month` \\| `year` | `month` | | × |\n| validRange | To set valid range | \\[[dayjs](https://day.js.org/), [dayjs](https://day.js.org/)] | - | | × |\n| value | The current selected date | [dayjs](https://day.js.org/) | - | | × |\n| onChange | Callback for when date changes | function(date: Dayjs) | - | | × |\n| onPanelChange | Callback for when panel changes | function(date: Dayjs, mode: string) | - | | × |\n| onSelect | Callback for when a date is selected, include source info | function(date: Dayjs, info: { source: 'year' \\| 'month' \\| 'date' \\| 'customize' }) | - | `info`: 5.6.0 | × |\n\n## Semantic DOM\n\nhttps://ant.design/components/calendar/semantic.md\n\n## Design Token\n\n## Component Token (Calendar)\n| Token Name | Description | Type | Default Value |\n| --- | --- | --- | --- |\n| fullBg | Background color of full calendar | string | #ffffff |\n| fullPanelBg | Background color of full calendar panel | string | #ffffff |\n| itemActiveBg | Background color of selected date item | string | #e6f4ff |\n| miniContentHeight | Height of mini calendar content | string \\| number | 256 |\n| monthControlWidth | Width of month select | string \\| number | 70 |\n| yearControlWidth | Width of year select | string \\| number | 80 |\n\n## Global Token\n| Token Name | Description | Type | Default Value |\n| --- | --- | --- | --- |\n| borderRadiusLG | LG size border radius, used in some large border radius components, such as Card, Modal and other components. | number | |\n| borderRadiusSM | SM size border radius, used in small size components, such as Button, Input, Select and other input components in small size | number | |\n| colorBgContainer | Container background color, e.g: default button, input box, etc. Be sure not to confuse this with `colorBgElevated`. | string | |\n| colorFillSecondary | The second level of fill color can outline the shape of the element more clearly, such as Rate, Skeleton, etc. It can also be used as the Hover state of the third level of fill color, such as Table, etc. | string | |\n| colorIcon | Weak action. Such as `allowClear` or Alert close button | string | |\n| colorIconHover | Weak action hover color. Such as `allowClear` or Alert close button | string | |\n| colorPrimary | Brand color is one of the most direct visual elements to reflect the characteristics and communication of the product. After you have selected the brand color, we will automatically generate a complete color palette and assign it effective design semantics. | string | |\n| colorSplit | Used as the color of separator, this color is the same as colorBorderSecondary but with transparency. | string | |\n| colorText | Default text color which comply with W3C standards, and this color is also the darkest neutral color. | string | |\n| colorTextDisabled | Control the color of text in disabled state. | string | |\n| colorTextHeading | Control the font color of heading. | string | |\n| colorTextLightSolid | Control the highlight color of text with background color, such as the text in Primary Button components. | string | |\n| colorTextTertiary | The third level of text color is generally used for descriptive text, such as form supplementary explanation text, list descriptive text, etc. | string | |\n| controlHeightLG | LG component height | number | |\n| controlHeightSM | SM component height | number | |\n| controlItemBgActive | Control the background color of control component item when active. | string | |\n| controlItemBgHover | Control the background color of control component item when hovering. | string | |\n| fontFamily | The font family of Ant Design prioritizes the default interface font of the system, and provides a set of alternative font libraries that are suitable for screen display to maintain the readability and readability of the font under different platforms and browsers, reflecting the friendly, stable and professional characteristics. | string | |\n| fontSize | The most widely used font size in the design system, from which the text gradient will be derived. | number | |\n| fontWeightStrong | Control the font weight of heading components (such as h1, h2, h3) or selected item. | number | |\n| lineHeight | Line height of text. | number | |\n| lineType | Border style of base components | string | |\n| lineWidth | Border width of base components | number | |\n| lineWidthBold | The default line width of the outline class components, such as Button, Input, Select, etc. | number | |\n| marginXS | Control the margin of an element, with a small size. | number | |\n| marginXXS | Control the margin of an element, with the smallest size. | number | |\n| motionDurationMid | Motion speed, medium speed. Used for medium element animation interaction. | string | |\n| motionDurationSlow | Motion speed, slow speed. Used for large element animation interaction. | string | |\n| padding | Control the padding of the element. | number | |\n| paddingSM | Control the small padding of the element. | number | |\n| paddingXS | Control the extra small padding of the element. | number | |\n| paddingXXS | Control the extra extra small padding of the element. | number | |\n| screenXS | Control the screen width of extra small screens. | number | |\n\n## FAQ\n\n### How to use Calendar with customize date library? {#faq-customize-date-library}\n\nSee [Use custom date library](/docs/react/use-custom-date-library#calendar)\n\n### How to set locale for date-related components? {#faq-set-locale-date-components}\n\nSee [How to set locale for date-related components](/components/date-picker/#localization)\n\n### Date-related components locale is not working? {#faq-locale-not-working}\n\nSee FAQ [Date-related-components-locale-is-not-working?](/docs/react/faq#date-related-components-locale-is-not-working)\n\n### How to get date from panel click? {#faq-get-date-panel-click}\n\n`onSelect` provide `info.source` to help on this:\n\n```tsx\n<Calendar\n  onSelect={(date, { source }) => {\n    if (source === 'date') {\n      console.log('Panel Select:', source);\n    }\n  }}\n/>\n```\n\n---\n\n## card\n\nSource: https://ant.design/components/card.md\n\n---\ncategory: Components\ngroup: Data Display\ntitle: Card\ndescription: A container for displaying information.\ncover: https://mdn.alipayobjects.com/huamei_7uahnr/afts/img/A*QXO1SKEdIzYAAAAAAAAAAAAADrJ8AQ/original\ncoverDark: https://mdn.alipayobjects.com/huamei_7uahnr/afts/img/A*5WDvQp_H7LUAAAAAAAAAAAAADrJ8AQ/original\n---\n\n## When To Use\n\nA card can be used to display content related to a single subject. The content can consist of multiple elements of varying types and sizes.\n\n## Examples\n\n### Basic card\n\nA basic card containing a title, content and an extra corner content. Supports two sizes: `medium` and `small`.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { Card, Space } from 'antd';\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <Space vertical size={16}>\n    <Card title=\"Default size card\" extra={<a href=\"#\">More</a>} style={{ width: 300 }}>\n      <p>Card content</p>\n      <p>Card content</p>\n      <p>Card content</p>\n    </Card>\n    <Card size=\"small\" title=\"Small size card\" extra={<a href=\"#\">More</a>} style={{ width: 300 }}>\n      <p>Card content</p>\n      <p>Card content</p>\n      <p>Card content</p>\n    </Card>\n  </Space>\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### No border\n\nA borderless card on a gray background.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { Card } from 'antd';\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <Card title=\"Card title\" variant=\"borderless\" style={{ width: 300 }}>\n    <p>Card content</p>\n    <p>Card content</p>\n    <p>Card content</p>\n  </Card>\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Simple card\n\nA simple card only containing a content area.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { Card } from 'antd';\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <Card style={{ width: 300 }}>\n    <p>Card content</p>\n    <p>Card content</p>\n    <p>Card content</p>\n  </Card>\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Customized content\n\nYou can use `Card.Meta` to support more flexible content.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { Card } from 'antd';\n\nconst { Meta } = Card;\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <Card\n    hoverable\n    variant=\"borderless\"\n    style={{ width: 240 }}\n    cover={\n      <img\n        draggable={false}\n        alt=\"example\"\n        src=\"https://os.alipayobjects.com/rmsportal/QBnOOoLaAfKPirc.png\"\n      />\n    }\n  >\n    <Meta title=\"Europe Street beat\" description=\"www.instagram.com\" />\n  </Card>\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Card in column\n\nCards usually cooperate with grid column layout in overview page.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { Card, Col, Row } from 'antd';\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <Row gutter={16}>\n    <Col span={8}>\n      <Card title=\"Card title\" variant=\"borderless\">\n        Card content\n      </Card>\n    </Col>\n    <Col span={8}>\n      <Card title=\"Card title\" variant=\"borderless\">\n        Card content\n      </Card>\n    </Col>\n    <Col span={8}>\n      <Card title=\"Card title\" variant=\"borderless\">\n        Card content\n      </Card>\n    </Col>\n  </Row>\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Loading card\n\nShows a loading indicator while the contents of the card is being fetched.\n\n```tsx\nimport React, { useState } from 'react';\nimport { EditOutlined, EllipsisOutlined, SettingOutlined } from '@ant-design/icons';\nimport { Avatar, Card, Flex, Switch } from 'antd';\n\nconst actions: React.ReactNode[] = [\n  <EditOutlined key=\"edit\" />,\n  <SettingOutlined key=\"setting\" />,\n  <EllipsisOutlined key=\"ellipsis\" />,\n];\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => {\n  const [loading, setLoading] = useState<boolean>(true);\n  return (\n    <Flex gap=\"medium\" align=\"start\" vertical>\n      <Switch checked={!loading} onChange={(checked) => setLoading(!checked)} />\n      <Card loading={loading} actions={actions} style={{ minWidth: 300 }}>\n        <Card.Meta\n          avatar={<Avatar src=\"https://api.dicebear.com/10.x/lorelei/svg?seed=1\" />}\n          title=\"Card title\"\n          description={\n            <>\n              <p>This is the description</p>\n              <p>This is the description</p>\n            </>\n          }\n        />\n      </Card>\n      <Card loading={loading} actions={actions} style={{ minWidth: 300 }}>\n        <Card.Meta\n          avatar={<Avatar src=\"https://api.dicebear.com/10.x/lorelei/svg?seed=2\" />}\n          title=\"Card title\"\n          description={\n            <>\n              <p>This is the description</p>\n              <p>This is the description</p>\n            </>\n          }\n        />\n      </Card>\n    </Flex>\n  );\n};\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Grid card\n\nGrid style card content.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { Card } from 'antd';\n\nconst gridStyle: React.CSSProperties = {\n  width: '25%',\n  textAlign: 'center',\n};\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <Card title=\"Card Title\">\n    <Card.Grid style={gridStyle}>Content</Card.Grid>\n    <Card.Grid hoverable={false} style={gridStyle}>\n      Content\n    </Card.Grid>\n    <Card.Grid style={gridStyle}>Content</Card.Grid>\n    <Card.Grid style={gridStyle}>Content</Card.Grid>\n    <Card.Grid style={gridStyle}>Content</Card.Grid>\n    <Card.Grid style={gridStyle}>Content</Card.Grid>\n    <Card.Grid style={gridStyle}>Content</Card.Grid>\n  </Card>\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Inner card\n\nIt can be placed inside the ordinary card to display the information of the multilevel structure.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { Card } from 'antd';\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <Card title=\"Card title\">\n    <Card type=\"inner\" title=\"Inner Card title\" extra={<a href=\"#\">More</a>}>\n      Inner Card content\n    </Card>\n    <Card\n      style={{ marginTop: 16 }}\n      type=\"inner\"\n      title=\"Inner Card title\"\n      extra={<a href=\"#\">More</a>}\n    >\n      Inner Card content\n    </Card>\n  </Card>\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### With tabs\n\nMore content can be hosted.\n\n```tsx\nimport React, { useState } from 'react';\nimport { Card } from 'antd';\n\nconst tabList = [\n  {\n    key: 'tab1',\n    tab: 'tab1',\n  },\n  {\n    key: 'tab2',\n    tab: 'tab2',\n  },\n];\n\nconst contentList: Record<string, React.ReactNode> = {\n  tab1: <p>content1</p>,\n  tab2: <p>content2</p>,\n};\n\nconst tabListNoTitle = [\n  {\n    key: 'article',\n    label: 'article',\n  },\n  {\n    key: 'app',\n    label: 'app',\n  },\n  {\n    key: 'project',\n    label: 'project',\n  },\n];\n\nconst contentListNoTitle: Record<string, React.ReactNode> = {\n  article: <p>article content</p>,\n  app: <p>app content</p>,\n  project: <p>project content</p>,\n};\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => {\n  const [activeTabKey1, setActiveTabKey1] = useState<string>('tab1');\n  const [activeTabKey2, setActiveTabKey2] = useState<string>('app');\n\n  const onTab1Change = (key: string) => {\n    setActiveTabKey1(key);\n  };\n  const onTab2Change = (key: string) => {\n    setActiveTabKey2(key);\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <>\n      <Card\n        style={{ width: '100%' }}\n        title=\"Card title\"\n        extra={<a href=\"#\">More</a>}\n        tabList={tabList}\n        activeTabKey={activeTabKey1}\n        onTabChange={onTab1Change}\n      >\n        {contentList[activeTabKey1]}\n      </Card>\n      <br />\n      <br />\n      <Card\n        style={{ width: '100%' }}\n        tabList={tabListNoTitle}\n        activeTabKey={activeTabKey2}\n        tabBarExtraContent={<a href=\"#\">More</a>}\n        onTabChange={onTab2Change}\n        tabProps={{ size: 'medium' }}\n      >\n        {contentListNoTitle[activeTabKey2]}\n      </Card>\n    </>\n  );\n};\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Support more content configuration\n\nA Card that supports `cover`, `avatar`, `title` and `description`.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { EditOutlined, EllipsisOutlined, SettingOutlined } from '@ant-design/icons';\nimport { Avatar, Card } from 'antd';\n\nconst { Meta } = Card;\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <Card\n    style={{ width: 300 }}\n    cover={\n      <img\n        draggable={false}\n        alt=\"example\"\n        src=\"https://gw.alipayobjects.com/zos/rmsportal/JiqGstEfoWAOHiTxclqi.png\"\n      />\n    }\n    actions={[\n      <SettingOutlined key=\"setting\" />,\n      <EditOutlined key=\"edit\" />,\n      <EllipsisOutlined key=\"ellipsis\" />,\n    ]}\n  >\n    <Meta\n      avatar={<Avatar src=\"https://api.dicebear.com/10.x/lorelei/svg?seed=8\" />}\n      title=\"Card title\"\n      description=\"This is the description\"\n    />\n  </Card>\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Custom semantic dom styling\n\nYou can customize the [semantic dom](#semantic-dom) style of Card by passing objects/functions through `classNames` and `styles`.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { EditOutlined, HeartOutlined, ShareAltOutlined } from '@ant-design/icons';\nimport { Avatar, Button, Card, Flex } from 'antd';\nimport type { CardMetaProps, CardProps, GetProp } from 'antd';\nimport { createStyles } from 'antd-style';\n\nconst { Meta } = Card;\n\nconst useStyles = createStyles(({ token }) => ({\n  root: {\n    width: 300,\n    backgroundColor: token.colorBgContainer,\n    borderRadius: token.borderRadius,\n    boxShadow: '0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.1)',\n    border: `1px solid ${token.colorBorderSecondary}`,\n  },\n  header: {\n    borderBottom: 'none',\n    paddingBottom: 8,\n  },\n  body: {\n    paddingTop: 0,\n  },\n}));\n\nconst stylesCard: CardProps['styles'] = {\n  root: {\n    boxShadow: '0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.06)',\n    borderRadius: 8,\n  },\n  title: {\n    fontSize: 16,\n    fontWeight: 500,\n  },\n};\n\nconst stylesCardFn: CardProps['styles'] = (info): GetProp<CardProps, 'styles', 'Return'> => {\n  if (info.props.variant === 'outlined') {\n    return {\n      root: {\n        borderColor: '#696FC7',\n        boxShadow: '0 2px 8px #A7AAE1',\n        borderRadius: 8,\n      },\n      extra: {\n        color: '#696FC7',\n      },\n      title: {\n        fontSize: 16,\n        fontWeight: 500,\n        color: '#A7AAE1',\n      },\n    };\n  }\n};\n\nconst stylesCardMeta: CardMetaProps['styles'] = {\n  title: {\n    color: '#A7AAE1',\n  },\n  description: {\n    color: '#A7AAE1',\n  },\n};\n\nconst actions = [\n  <HeartOutlined key=\"heart\" style={{ color: '#ff6b6b' }} />,\n  <ShareAltOutlined key=\"share\" style={{ color: '#4ecdc4' }} />,\n  <EditOutlined key=\"edit\" style={{ color: '#45b7d1' }} />,\n];\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => {\n  const { styles: classNames } = useStyles();\n\n  const sharedCardProps: CardProps = {\n    classNames,\n    actions,\n  };\n\n  const sharedCardMetaProps: CardMetaProps = {\n    avatar: <Avatar src=\"https://api.dicebear.com/10.x/lorelei/svg?seed=1\" />,\n    description: 'This is the description',\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <Flex gap=\"medium\">\n      <Card\n        {...sharedCardProps}\n        title=\"Object Card\"\n        styles={stylesCard}\n        extra={<Button type=\"link\">More</Button>}\n        variant=\"borderless\"\n      >\n        <Meta {...sharedCardMetaProps} title=\"Object Card Meta title\" />\n      </Card>\n      <Card\n        {...sharedCardProps}\n        title=\"Function Card\"\n        styles={stylesCardFn}\n        extra={\n          <Button type=\"link\" styles={{ root: { color: '#A7AAE1' } }}>\n            More\n          </Button>\n        }\n      >\n        <Meta {...sharedCardMetaProps} styles={stylesCardMeta} title=\"Function Card Meta title\" />\n      </Card>\n    </Flex>\n  );\n};\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n## API\n\nCommon props ref：[Common props](/docs/react/common-props)\n\n```jsx\n<Card title=\"Card title\">Card content</Card>\n```\n\n| Property | Description | Type | Default | Version | [Global Config](/components/config-provider#component-config) |\n| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |\n| actions | The action list, shows at the bottom of the Card | Array<ReactNode> | - | | × |\n| activeTabKey | Current TabPane's key | string | - | | × |\n| ~~bordered~~ | Toggles rendering of the border around the card, please use `variant` instead | boolean | true | | × |\n| ~~bodyStyle~~ | Style of card body, please use `styles.body` instead | CSSProperties | - | - | × |\n| variant | Variants of Card | `outlined` \\| `borderless` | `outlined` | 5.24.0 | 5.24.0 |\n| classNames | Customize class for each semantic structure inside the component. Supports object or function. | Record<[SemanticDOM](#semantic-dom), string> \\| (info: { props })=> Record<[SemanticDOM](#semantic-dom), string> | - | | 5.14.0 |\n| cover | Card cover | ReactNode | - | | × |\n| defaultActiveTabKey | Initial active TabPane's key, if `activeTabKey` is not set | string | `The key of first tab` | | × |\n| extra | Content to render in the top-right corner of the card | ReactNode | - | | × |\n| hoverable | Lift up when hovering card | boolean | false | | × |\n| ~~headStyle~~ | Style of card head, please use `styles.header` instead | CSSProperties | - | - | × |\n| loading | Shows a loading indicator while the contents of the card are being fetched | boolean | false | | × |\n| size | Size of card | `medium` \\| `small` | `medium` | | × |\n| tabBarExtraContent | Extra content in tab bar | ReactNode | - | | × |\n| tabList | List of TabPane's head | [TabItemType](/components/tabs#tabitemtype)[] | - | | × |\n| tabProps | [Tabs](/components/tabs/#tabs) | - | - | | × |\n| title | Card title | ReactNode | - | | × |\n| type | Card style type, can be set to `inner` or not set | string | - | | × |\n| styles | Customize inline style for each semantic structure inside the component. Supports object or function. | Record<[SemanticDOM](#semantic-dom), CSSProperties> \\| (info: { props })=> Record<[SemanticDOM](#semantic-dom), CSSProperties> | - | | 5.14.0 |\n| onTabChange | Callback when tab is switched | (key) => void | - | | × |\n\n### Card.Grid\n\n| Property | Description | Type | Default | Version |\n| --------- | ------------------------------- | ------- | ------- | ------- |\n| hoverable | Lift up when hovering card grid | boolean | true | |\n\n### Card.Meta\n\n| Property | Description | Type | Default | Version | [Global Config](/components/config-provider#component-config) |\n| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |\n| avatar | Avatar or icon | ReactNode | - | | × |\n| description | Description content | ReactNode | - | | × |\n| title | Title content | ReactNode | - | | × |\n\n## Semantic DOM\n\n### Card\n\nhttps://ant.design/components/card/semantic.md\n\n### Card.Meta\n\nhttps://ant.design/components/card/semantic_meta.md\n\n## Design Token\n\n## Component Token (Card)\n| Token Name | Description | Type | Default Value |\n| --- | --- | --- | --- |\n| actionsBg | Background color of card actions | string | #ffffff |\n| actionsLiMargin | Margin of each item in card actions | string | 12px 0 |\n| bodyPadding | Padding of card body | number | 24 |\n| bodyPaddingSM | Padding of small card body | number | 12 |\n| extraColor | Text color of extra area | string | rgba(0,0,0,0.88) |\n| headerBg | Background color of card header | string | transparent |\n| headerFontSize | Font size of card header | string \\| number | 16 |\n| headerFontSizeSM | Font size of small card header | string \\| number | 14 |\n| headerHeight | Height of card header | string \\| number | 56 |\n| headerHeightSM | Height of small card header | string \\| number | 38 |\n| headerPadding | Padding of card head | number | 24 |\n| headerPaddingSM | Padding of small card head | number | 12 |\n| tabsMarginBottom | Margin bottom of tabs component | number | -17 |\n\n## Global Token\n| Token Name | Description | Type | Default Value |\n| --- | --- | --- | --- |\n| borderRadiusLG | LG size border radius, used in some large border radius components, such as Card, Modal and other components. | number | |\n| boxShadowTertiary | Control the tertiary box shadow style of an element. | string | |\n| colorBgContainer | Container background color, e.g: default button, input box, etc. Be sure not to confuse this with `colorBgElevated`. | string | |\n| colorBorderSecondary | Slightly lighter than the default border color, this color is the same as `colorSplit`. Solid color is used. | string | |\n| colorFillAlter | Control the alternative background color of element. | string | |\n| colorIcon | Weak action. Such as `allowClear` or Alert close button | string | |\n| colorPrimary | Brand color is one of the most direct visual elements to reflect the characteristics and communication of the product. After you have selected the brand color, we will automatically generate a complete color palette and assign it effective design semantics. | string | |\n| colorText | Default text color which comply with W3C standards, and this color is also the darkest neutral color. | string | |\n| colorTextDescription | Control the font color of text description. | string | |\n| colorTextHeading | Control the font color of heading. | string | |\n| fontFamily | The font family of Ant Design prioritizes the default interface font of the system, and provides a set of alternative font libraries that are suitable for screen display to maintain the readability and readability of the font under different platforms and browsers, reflecting the friendly, stable and professional characteristics. | string | |\n| fontSize | The most widely used font size in the design system, from which the text gradient will be derived. | number | |\n| fontSizeLG | Large font size | number | |\n| fontWeightStrong | Control the font weight of heading components (such as h1, h2, h3) or selected item. | number | |\n| lineHeight | Line height of text. | number | |\n| lineType | Border style of base components | string | |\n| lineWidth | Border width of base components | number | |\n| marginXS | Control the margin of an element, with a small size. | number | |\n| marginXXS | Control the margin of an element, with the smallest size. | number | |\n| motionDurationMid | Motion speed, medium speed. Used for medium element animation interaction. | string | |\n| padding | Control the padding of the element. | number | |\n| paddingLG | Control the large padding of the element. | number | |\n\n---\n\n## carousel\n\nSource: https://ant.design/components/carousel.md\n\n---\ncategory: Components\ngroup: Data Display\ntitle: Carousel\ndescription: A set of carousel areas.\ncover: https://mdn.alipayobjects.com/huamei_7uahnr/afts/img/A*bPMSSqbaTMkAAAAAAAAAAAAADrJ8AQ/original\ncoverDark: https://mdn.alipayobjects.com/huamei_7uahnr/afts/img/A*a-58QpYnqOsAAAAAAAAAAAAADrJ8AQ/original\ndemo:\n cols: 2\n---\n\n## When To Use\n\n- When there is a group of content on the same level.\n- When there is insufficient content space, it can be used to save space in the form of a revolving door.\n- Commonly used for a group of pictures/cards.\n\n## Examples\n\n### Basic\n\nBasic usage.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { Carousel } from 'antd';\n\nconst contentStyle: React.CSSProperties = {\n  margin: 0,\n  height: '160px',\n  color: '#fff',\n  lineHeight: '160px',\n  textAlign: 'center',\n  background: '#364d79',\n};\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => {\n  const onChange = (currentSlide: number) => {\n    console.log(currentSlide);\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <Carousel afterChange={onChange}>\n      <div>\n        <h3 style={contentStyle}>1</h3>\n      </div>\n      <div>\n        <h3 style={contentStyle}>2</h3>\n      </div>\n      <div>\n        <h3 style={contentStyle}>3</h3>\n      </div>\n      <div>\n        <h3 style={contentStyle}>4</h3>\n      </div>\n    </Carousel>\n  );\n};\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Position\n\nThere are 4 position options available.\n\n```tsx\nimport React, { useState } from 'react';\nimport type { CarouselProps, RadioChangeEvent } from 'antd';\nimport { Carousel, Radio } from 'antd';\n\ntype DotPlacement = CarouselProps['dotPlacement'];\n\nconst contentStyle: React.CSSProperties = {\n  margin: 0,\n  height: '160px',\n  color: '#fff',\n  lineHeight: '160px',\n  textAlign: 'center',\n  background: '#364d79',\n};\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => {\n  const [dotPlacement, setDotPlacement] = useState<DotPlacement>('top');\n\n  const handlePositionChange = ({ target: { value } }: RadioChangeEvent) => {\n    setDotPlacement(value);\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <>\n      <Radio.Group onChange={handlePositionChange} value={dotPlacement} style={{ marginBottom: 8 }}>\n        <Radio.Button value=\"top\">Top</Radio.Button>\n        <Radio.Button value=\"bottom\">Bottom</Radio.Button>\n        <Radio.Button value=\"start\">Start</Radio.Button>\n        <Radio.Button value=\"end\">End</Radio.Button>\n      </Radio.Group>\n      <Carousel dotPlacement={dotPlacement}>\n        <div>\n          <h3 style={contentStyle}>1</h3>\n        </div>\n        <div>\n          <h3 style={contentStyle}>2</h3>\n        </div>\n        <div>\n          <h3 style={contentStyle}>3</h3>\n        </div>\n        <div>\n          <h3 style={contentStyle}>4</h3>\n        </div>\n      </Carousel>\n    </>\n  );\n};\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Scroll automatically\n\nTiming of scrolling to the next card/picture.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { Carousel } from 'antd';\n\nconst contentStyle: React.CSSProperties = {\n  margin: 0,\n  height: '160px',\n  color: '#fff',\n  lineHeight: '160px',\n  textAlign: 'center',\n  background: '#364d79',\n};\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <Carousel autoplay>\n    <div>\n      <h3 style={contentStyle}>1</h3>\n    </div>\n    <div>\n      <h3 style={contentStyle}>2</h3>\n    </div>\n    <div>\n      <h3 style={contentStyle}>3</h3>\n    </div>\n    <div>\n      <h3 style={contentStyle}>4</h3>\n    </div>\n  </Carousel>\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Fade in\n\nSlides use fade for transition.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { Carousel } from 'antd';\n\nconst contentStyle: React.CSSProperties = {\n  margin: 0,\n  height: '160px',\n  color: '#fff',\n  lineHeight: '160px',\n  textAlign: 'center',\n  background: '#364d79',\n};\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <Carousel effect=\"fade\">\n    <div>\n      <h3 style={contentStyle}>1</h3>\n    </div>\n    <div>\n      <h3 style={contentStyle}>2</h3>\n    </div>\n    <div>\n      <h3 style={contentStyle}>3</h3>\n    </div>\n    <div>\n      <h3 style={contentStyle}>4</h3>\n    </div>\n  </Carousel>\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Arrows for switching\n\nShow the arrows for switching.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { Carousel } from 'antd';\n\nconst contentStyle: React.CSSProperties = {\n  margin: 0,\n  height: '160px',\n  color: '#fff',\n  lineHeight: '160px',\n  textAlign: 'center',\n  background: '#364d79',\n};\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <>\n    <Carousel arrows infinite={false}>\n      <div>\n        <h3 style={contentStyle}>1</h3>\n      </div>\n      <div>\n        <h3 style={contentStyle}>2</h3>\n      </div>\n      <div>\n        <h3 style={contentStyle}>3</h3>\n      </div>\n      <div>\n        <h3 style={contentStyle}>4</h3>\n      </div>\n    </Carousel>\n    <br />\n    <Carousel arrows dotPlacement=\"start\" infinite={false}>\n      <div>\n        <h3 style={contentStyle}>1</h3>\n      </div>\n      <div>\n        <h3 style={contentStyle}>2</h3>\n      </div>\n      <div>\n        <h3 style={contentStyle}>3</h3>\n      </div>\n      <div>\n        <h3 style={contentStyle}>4</h3>\n      </div>\n    </Carousel>\n  </>\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Progress of dots\n\nShow progress of dots.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { Carousel } from 'antd';\n\nconst contentStyle: React.CSSProperties = {\n  margin: 0,\n  height: '160px',\n  color: '#fff',\n  lineHeight: '160px',\n  textAlign: 'center',\n  background: '#364d79',\n};\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <Carousel autoplay={{ dotDuration: true }} autoplaySpeed={5000}>\n    <div>\n      <h3 style={contentStyle}>1</h3>\n    </div>\n    <div>\n      <h3 style={contentStyle}>2</h3>\n    </div>\n    <div>\n      <h3 style={contentStyle}>3</h3>\n    </div>\n    <div>\n      <h3 style={contentStyle}>4</h3>\n    </div>\n  </Carousel>\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n## API\n\nCommon props ref：[Common props](/docs/react/common-props)\n\n| Property | Description | Type | Default | Version | [Global Config](/components/config-provider#component-config) |\n| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |\n| arrows | Whether to show switch arrows | boolean | false | 5.17.0 | × |\n| autoplay | Whether to scroll automatically, you can specify `autoplay={{ dotDuration: true }}` to display the progress bar | boolean \\| { dotDuration?: boolean } | false | dotDuration: 5.24.0 | × |\n| autoplaySpeed | Delay between each auto scroll (in milliseconds) | number | 3000 | | × |\n| adaptiveHeight | Adjust the slide's height automatically | boolean | false | | × |\n| dotPlacement | The position of the dots, which can be one of `top` `bottom` `start` `end` | string | `bottom` | | × |\n| ~~dotPosition~~ | The position of the dots, which can be one of `top` `bottom` `left` `right` `start` `end`, Please use `dotPlacement` instead | string | `bottom` | | × |\n| dots | Whether to show the dots at the bottom of the gallery, `object` for `dotsClass` | boolean \\| { className?: string } | true | | × |\n| draggable | Enable scrollable via dragging on desktop | boolean | false | | × |\n| fade | Whether to use fade transition | boolean | false | | × |\n| infinite | Infinitely wrap around contents | boolean | true | | × |\n| speed | Animation speed in milliseconds | number | 500 | | × |\n| easing | Transition interpolation function name | string | `linear` | | × |\n| effect | Transition effect | `scrollx` \\| `fade` | `scrollx` | | × |\n| afterChange | Callback function called after the current index changes | (current: number) => void | - | | × |\n| beforeChange | Callback function called before the current index changes | (current: number, next: number) => void | - | | × |\n| waitForAnimate | Whether to wait for the animation when switching | boolean | false | | × |\n\nFind more APIs in react-slick [documentation](https://react-slick.neostack.com/docs/api).\n\n## Methods\n\n| Name | Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| goTo(slideNumber, dontAnimate) | Go to slide index, if dontAnimate=true, it happens without animation |\n| next() | Change current slide to next slide |\n| prev() | Change current slide to previous slide |\n\n## Design Token\n\n## Component Token (Carousel)\n| Token Name | Description | Type | Default Value |\n| --- | --- | --- | --- |\n| arrowOffset | arrows offset to Carousel edge | number | 8 |\n| arrowSize | Size of arrows | number | 16 |\n| dotActiveWidth | Width of active indicator | string \\| number | 24 |\n| dotGap | gap between indicator | number | 4 |\n| dotHeight | Height of indicator | string \\| number | 3 |\n| dotOffset | dot offset to Carousel edge | number | 12 |\n| dotWidth | Width of indicator | string \\| number | 16 |\n\n## Global Token\n| Token Name | Description | Type | Default Value |\n| --- | --- | --- | --- |\n| colorBgContainer | Container background color, e.g: default button, input box, etc. Be sure not to confuse this with `colorBgElevated`. | string | |\n| colorText | Default text color which comply with W3C standards, and this color is also the darkest neutral color. | string | |\n| fontFamily | The font family of Ant Design prioritizes the default interface font of the system, and provides a set of alternative font libraries that are suitable for screen display to maintain the readability and readability of the font under different platforms and browsers, reflecting the friendly, stable and professional characteristics. | string | |\n| fontSize | The most widely used font size in the design system, from which the text gradient will be derived. | number | |\n| lineHeight | Line height of text. | number | |\n| marginXXS | Control the margin of an element, with the smallest size. | number | |\n| motionDurationSlow | Motion speed, slow speed. Used for large element animation interaction. | string | |\n\n## FAQ\n\n### How to add custom arrows? {#faq-add-custom-arrows}\n\nSee [#12479](https://github.com/ant-design/ant-design/issues/12479).\n\n---\n\n## cascader\n\nSource: https://ant.design/components/cascader.md\n\n---\ncategory: Components\ngroup: Data Entry\ntitle: Cascader\ndescription: Cascade selection box.\ncover: https://mdn.alipayobjects.com/huamei_7uahnr/afts/img/A*ngTnQZNOcK0AAAAAAAAAAAAADrJ8AQ/original\ncoverDark: https://mdn.alipayobjects.com/huamei_7uahnr/afts/img/A*Nt8xR7afyr0AAAAAAAAAAAAADrJ8AQ/original\ndemo:\n cols: 2\n---\n\n## When To Use\n\n- When you need to select from a set of associated data set. Such as province/city/district, company level, things classification.\n- When selecting from a large data set, with multi-stage classifications separated for easy selection.\n- Chooses cascade items in one float layer for better user experience.\n\n## Examples\n\n### Basic\n\nCascade selection box for selecting province/city/district.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport type { CascaderProps } from 'antd';\nimport { Cascader } from 'antd';\nimport type { HTMLAriaDataAttributes } from 'antd/es/_util/aria-data-attrs';\n\ntype Option = {\n  value: string;\n  label: string;\n  children?: Option[];\n} & HTMLAriaDataAttributes;\n\nconst options: Option[] = [\n  {\n    value: 'zhejiang',\n    label: 'Zhejiang',\n    'aria-label': 'Zhejiang',\n    'data-title': 'Zhejiang',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'hangzhou',\n        label: 'Hangzhou',\n        'aria-label': 'Hangzhou',\n        'data-title': 'Hangzhou',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'xihu',\n            label: 'West Lake',\n            'aria-label': 'West Lake',\n            'data-title': 'West Lake',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'jiangsu',\n    label: 'Jiangsu',\n    'aria-label': 'Jiangsu',\n    'data-title': 'Jiangsu',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'nanjing',\n        label: 'Nanjing',\n        'aria-label': 'Nanjing',\n        'data-title': 'Nanjing',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'zhonghuamen',\n            label: 'Zhong Hua Men',\n            'aria-label': 'Zhong Hua Men',\n            'data-title': 'Zhong Hua Men',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n];\n\nconst onChange: CascaderProps<Option>['onChange'] = (value) => {\n  console.log(value);\n};\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <Cascader options={options} onChange={onChange} placeholder=\"Please select\" />\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Default value\n\nSpecifies default value by an array.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport type { CascaderProps } from 'antd';\nimport { Cascader } from 'antd';\n\ninterface Option {\n  value: string;\n  label: string;\n  children?: Option[];\n}\n\nconst options: Option[] = [\n  {\n    value: 'zhejiang',\n    label: 'Zhejiang',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'hangzhou',\n        label: 'Hangzhou',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'xihu',\n            label: 'West Lake',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'jiangsu',\n    label: 'Jiangsu',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'nanjing',\n        label: 'Nanjing',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'zhonghuamen',\n            label: 'Zhong Hua Men',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n];\n\nconst onChange: CascaderProps<Option>['onChange'] = (value) => {\n  console.log(value);\n};\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <Cascader defaultValue={['zhejiang', 'hangzhou', 'xihu']} options={options} onChange={onChange} />\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Custom trigger\n\nSeparate trigger button and result.\n\n```tsx\nimport React, { useState } from 'react';\nimport type { CascaderProps } from 'antd';\nimport { Cascader } from 'antd';\n\ninterface Option {\n  value: string;\n  label: string;\n  children?: Option[];\n}\n\nconst options: Option[] = [\n  {\n    value: 'zhejiang',\n    label: 'Zhejiang',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'hangzhou',\n        label: 'Hangzhou',\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'jiangsu',\n    label: 'Jiangsu',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'nanjing',\n        label: 'Nanjing',\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n];\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => {\n  const [text, setText] = useState('Unselect');\n\n  const onChange: CascaderProps<Option>['onChange'] = (_, selectedOptions) => {\n    setText(selectedOptions.map((o) => o.label).join(', '));\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <span>\n      {text}\n       \n      <Cascader options={options} onChange={onChange}>\n        <a>Change city</a>\n      </Cascader>\n    </span>\n  );\n};\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Hover\n\nHover to expand sub menu, click to select option.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport type { CascaderProps } from 'antd';\nimport { Cascader } from 'antd';\n\ninterface Option {\n  value: string;\n  label: string;\n  children?: Option[];\n}\n\nconst options: Option[] = [\n  {\n    value: 'zhejiang',\n    label: 'Zhejiang',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'hangzhou',\n        label: 'Hangzhou',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'xihu',\n            label: 'West Lake',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'jiangsu',\n    label: 'Jiangsu',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'nanjing',\n        label: 'Nanjing',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'zhonghuamen',\n            label: 'Zhong Hua Men',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n];\n\nconst onChange: CascaderProps<Option>['onChange'] = (value) => {\n  console.log(value);\n};\n\n// Just show the latest item.\nconst displayRender = (labels: string[]) => labels[labels.length - 1];\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <Cascader\n    options={options}\n    expandTrigger=\"hover\"\n    displayRender={displayRender}\n    onChange={onChange}\n  />\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Disabled option\n\nDisable option by specifying the `disabled` property in `options`.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport type { CascaderProps } from 'antd';\nimport { Cascader } from 'antd';\n\ninterface Option {\n  value: string;\n  label: string;\n  disabled?: boolean;\n  children?: Option[];\n}\n\nconst options: Option[] = [\n  {\n    value: 'zhejiang',\n    label: 'Zhejiang',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'hangzhou',\n        label: 'Hangzhou',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'xihu',\n            label: 'West Lake',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'jiangsu',\n    label: 'Jiangsu',\n    disabled: true,\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'nanjing',\n        label: 'Nanjing',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'zhonghuamen',\n            label: 'Zhong Hua Men',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n];\n\nconst onChange: CascaderProps<Option>['onChange'] = (value) => {\n  console.log(value);\n};\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => <Cascader options={options} onChange={onChange} />;\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Change on select\n\nAllows the selection of only parent options.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport type { CascaderProps } from 'antd';\nimport { Cascader } from 'antd';\n\ninterface Option {\n  value: string;\n  label: string;\n  children?: Option[];\n}\n\nconst options: Option[] = [\n  {\n    value: 'zhejiang',\n    label: 'Zhejiang',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'hangzhou',\n        label: 'Hanzhou',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'xihu',\n            label: 'West Lake',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'jiangsu',\n    label: 'Jiangsu',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'nanjing',\n        label: 'Nanjing',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'zhonghuamen',\n            label: 'Zhong Hua Men',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n];\n\nconst onChange: CascaderProps<Option>['onChange'] = (value) => {\n  console.log(value);\n};\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => <Cascader options={options} onChange={onChange} changeOnSelect />;\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Multiple\n\nSelect multiple options. Disable the `checkbox` by adding the `disableCheckbox` property and selecting a specific item. The style of the disable can be modified by the className.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport type { CascaderProps } from 'antd';\nimport { Cascader } from 'antd';\n\ninterface Option {\n  value: string | number;\n  label: string;\n  children?: Option[];\n  disableCheckbox?: boolean;\n}\n\nconst options: Option[] = [\n  {\n    label: 'Light',\n    value: 'light',\n    children: Array.from({ length: 20 }).map((_, index) => ({\n      label: `Number ${index}`,\n      value: index,\n    })),\n  },\n  {\n    label: 'Bamboo',\n    value: 'bamboo',\n    children: [\n      {\n        label: 'Little',\n        value: 'little',\n        children: [\n          {\n            label: 'Toy Fish',\n            value: 'fish',\n            disableCheckbox: true,\n          },\n          {\n            label: 'Toy Cards',\n            value: 'cards',\n          },\n          {\n            label: 'Toy Bird',\n            value: 'bird',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n];\n\nconst onChange: CascaderProps<Option, 'value', true>['onChange'] = (value) => {\n  console.log(value);\n};\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <Cascader\n    style={{ width: '100%' }}\n    options={options}\n    onChange={onChange}\n    multiple\n    maxTagCount=\"responsive\"\n  />\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### ShowCheckedStrategy\n\nShows a selected item in a box using `showCheckedStrategy`.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport type { CascaderProps } from 'antd';\nimport { Cascader } from 'antd';\n\nconst { SHOW_CHILD } = Cascader;\n\ninterface Option {\n  value: string | number;\n  label: string;\n  children?: Option[];\n}\nconst options: Option[] = [\n  {\n    label: 'Light',\n    value: 'light',\n    children: Array.from({ length: 20 }).map((_, index) => ({\n      label: `Number ${index}`,\n      value: index,\n    })),\n  },\n  {\n    label: 'Bamboo',\n    value: 'bamboo',\n    children: [\n      {\n        label: 'Little',\n        value: 'little',\n        children: [\n          {\n            label: 'Toy Fish',\n            value: 'fish',\n          },\n          {\n            label: 'Toy Cards',\n            value: 'cards',\n          },\n          {\n            label: 'Toy Bird',\n            value: 'bird',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n];\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => {\n  const onChange: CascaderProps<Option, 'value', true>['onChange'] = (value) => {\n    console.log(value);\n  };\n  return (\n    <>\n      <Cascader\n        style={{ width: '100%' }}\n        options={options}\n        onChange={onChange}\n        multiple\n        maxTagCount=\"responsive\"\n        showCheckedStrategy={SHOW_CHILD}\n        defaultValue={[\n          ['bamboo', 'little', 'fish'],\n          ['bamboo', 'little', 'cards'],\n          ['bamboo', 'little', 'bird'],\n        ]}\n      />\n      <br />\n      <br />\n      <Cascader\n        style={{ width: '100%' }}\n        options={options}\n        onChange={onChange}\n        multiple\n        maxTagCount=\"responsive\"\n        defaultValue={[['bamboo']]}\n      />\n    </>\n  );\n};\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Size\n\nCascade selection box of different sizes.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport type { CascaderProps } from 'antd';\nimport { Cascader } from 'antd';\n\ninterface Option {\n  value: string;\n  label: string;\n  children?: Option[];\n}\n\nconst options: Option[] = [\n  {\n    value: 'zhejiang',\n    label: 'Zhejiang',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'hangzhou',\n        label: 'Hangzhou',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'xihu',\n            label: 'West Lake',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'jiangsu',\n    label: 'Jiangsu',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'nanjing',\n        label: 'Nanjing',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'zhonghuamen',\n            label: 'Zhong Hua Men',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n];\n\nconst onChange: CascaderProps<Option>['onChange'] = (value) => {\n  console.log(value);\n};\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <>\n    <Cascader size=\"large\" options={options} onChange={onChange} />\n    <br />\n    <br />\n    <Cascader options={options} onChange={onChange} />\n    <br />\n    <br />\n    <Cascader size=\"small\" options={options} onChange={onChange} />\n    <br />\n    <br />\n  </>\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Custom render\n\nFor instance, add an external link after the selected value.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { Cascader } from 'antd';\nimport type { CascaderProps, GetProp } from 'antd';\n\ntype DefaultOptionType = GetProp<CascaderProps, 'options'>[number];\n\ninterface Option {\n  value: string;\n  label: string;\n  children?: Option[];\n  code?: number;\n}\n\nconst options: Option[] = [\n  {\n    value: 'zhejiang',\n    label: 'Zhejiang',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'hangzhou',\n        label: 'Hangzhou',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'xihu',\n            label: 'West Lake',\n            code: 752100,\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'jiangsu',\n    label: 'Jiangsu',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'nanjing',\n        label: 'Nanjing',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'zhonghuamen',\n            label: 'Zhong Hua Men',\n            code: 453400,\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n];\n\nconst handleAreaClick = (\n  e: React.MouseEvent<HTMLAnchorElement>,\n  label: string,\n  option: DefaultOptionType,\n) => {\n  e.stopPropagation();\n  console.log('clicked', label, option);\n};\n\nconst displayRender: CascaderProps<Option>['displayRender'] = (labels, selectedOptions = []) =>\n  labels.map((label, i) => {\n    const option = selectedOptions[i];\n    if (i === labels.length - 1) {\n      return (\n        <span key={option.value}>\n          {label} (<a onClick={(e) => handleAreaClick(e, label, option)}>{option.code}</a>)\n        </span>\n      );\n    }\n    return <span key={option.value}>{label} / </span>;\n  });\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <Cascader\n    options={options}\n    defaultValue={['zhejiang', 'hangzhou', 'xihu']}\n    displayRender={displayRender}\n    style={{ width: '100%' }}\n    // `optionRender` is supported since 5.16.0\n    optionRender={(option) => (\n      <>\n        {option.label} ({option.value})\n      </>\n    )}\n  />\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Search\n\nSearch and select options directly.\n\n> Now, `Cascader[showSearch]` doesn't support search on server, more info [#5547](https://github.com/ant-design/ant-design/issues/5547)\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { Cascader } from 'antd';\nimport type { CascaderProps, GetProp } from 'antd';\n\ntype DefaultOptionType = GetProp<CascaderProps, 'options'>[number];\n\ninterface Option {\n  value: string;\n  label: string;\n  children?: Option[];\n  disabled?: boolean;\n}\n\nconst options: Option[] = [\n  {\n    value: 'zhejiang',\n    label: 'Zhejiang',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'hangzhou',\n        label: 'Hangzhou',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'xihu',\n            label: 'West Lake',\n          },\n          {\n            value: 'xiasha',\n            label: 'Xia Sha',\n            disabled: true,\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'jiangsu',\n    label: 'Jiangsu',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'nanjing',\n        label: 'Nanjing',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'zhonghuamen',\n            label: 'Zhong Hua men',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n];\n\nconst onChange: CascaderProps<Option>['onChange'] = (value, selectedOptions) => {\n  console.log(value, selectedOptions);\n};\n\nconst filter = (inputValue: string, path: DefaultOptionType[]) =>\n  path.some((option) => (option.label as string).toLowerCase().includes(inputValue.toLowerCase()));\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <Cascader\n    options={options}\n    onChange={onChange}\n    placeholder=\"Please select\"\n    showSearch={{ filter, onSearch: (value) => console.log(value) }}\n  />\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Load Options Lazily\n\nLoad options lazily with `loadData`.\n\n> Note: `loadData` cannot work with `showSearch`.\n\n```tsx\nimport React, { useState } from 'react';\nimport type { CascaderProps } from 'antd';\nimport { Cascader } from 'antd';\n\ninterface Option {\n  value?: string | number | null;\n  label: React.ReactNode;\n  children?: Option[];\n  isLeaf?: boolean;\n}\n\nconst optionLists: Option[] = [\n  {\n    value: 'zhejiang',\n    label: 'Zhejiang',\n    isLeaf: false,\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'jiangsu',\n    label: 'Jiangsu',\n    isLeaf: false,\n  },\n];\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => {\n  const [options, setOptions] = useState<Option[]>(optionLists);\n\n  const onChange: CascaderProps<Option>['onChange'] = (value, selectedOptions) => {\n    console.log(value, selectedOptions);\n  };\n\n  const loadData = (selectedOptions: Option[]) => {\n    const targetOption = selectedOptions[selectedOptions.length - 1];\n\n    // load options lazily\n    setTimeout(() => {\n      targetOption.children = [\n        {\n          label: `${targetOption.label} Dynamic 1`,\n          value: 'dynamic1',\n        },\n        {\n          label: `${targetOption.label} Dynamic 2`,\n          value: 'dynamic2',\n        },\n      ];\n      setOptions([...options]);\n    }, 1000);\n  };\n\n  return <Cascader options={options} loadData={loadData} onChange={onChange} changeOnSelect />;\n};\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Custom Field Names\n\nCustom field names.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport type { CascaderProps } from 'antd';\nimport { Cascader } from 'antd';\n\ninterface Option {\n  code: string;\n  name: string;\n  items?: Option[];\n}\n\nconst options: Option[] = [\n  {\n    code: 'zhejiang',\n    name: 'Zhejiang',\n    items: [\n      {\n        code: 'hangzhou',\n        name: 'Hangzhou',\n        items: [\n          {\n            code: 'xihu',\n            name: 'West Lake',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n  {\n    code: 'jiangsu',\n    name: 'Jiangsu',\n    items: [\n      {\n        code: 'nanjing',\n        name: 'Nanjing',\n        items: [\n          {\n            code: 'zhonghuamen',\n            name: 'Zhong Hua Men',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n];\n\nconst onChange: CascaderProps<Option>['onChange'] = (value) => {\n  console.log(value);\n};\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <Cascader\n    fieldNames={{ label: 'name', value: 'code', children: 'items' }}\n    options={options}\n    onChange={onChange}\n    placeholder=\"Please select\"\n  />\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Prefix and Suffix\n\nUse `prefix` to customize the prefix content, use `suffixIcon` to customize the selection box suffix icon, and use `expandIcon` to customize the current item expand icon.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { SmileOutlined } from '@ant-design/icons';\nimport type { CascaderProps } from 'antd';\nimport { Cascader } from 'antd';\n\ninterface Option {\n  value: string;\n  label: string;\n  children?: Option[];\n}\n\nconst options: Option[] = [\n  {\n    value: 'zhejiang',\n    label: 'Zhejiang',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'hangzhou',\n        label: 'Hangzhou',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'xihu',\n            label: 'West Lake',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'jiangsu',\n    label: 'Jiangsu',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'nanjing',\n        label: 'Nanjing',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'zhonghuamen',\n            label: 'Zhong Hua Men',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n];\n\nconst onChange: CascaderProps<Option>['onChange'] = (value) => {\n  console.log(value);\n};\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <>\n    <Cascader\n      suffixIcon={<SmileOutlined />}\n      options={options}\n      onChange={onChange}\n      placeholder=\"Please select\"\n    />\n    <br />\n    <br />\n    <Cascader suffixIcon=\"ab\" options={options} onChange={onChange} placeholder=\"Please select\" />\n    <br />\n    <br />\n    <Cascader\n      expandIcon={<SmileOutlined />}\n      options={options}\n      onChange={onChange}\n      placeholder=\"Please select\"\n    />\n    <br />\n    <br />\n    <Cascader expandIcon=\"ab\" options={options} onChange={onChange} placeholder=\"Please select\" />\n    <br />\n    <br />\n    <Cascader\n      prefix={<SmileOutlined />}\n      options={options}\n      onChange={onChange}\n      placeholder=\"Please select\"\n    />\n  </>\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Custom dropdown\n\nCustomize the dropdown menu via `popupRender`.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { Cascader, Divider } from 'antd';\n\ninterface Option {\n  value: string;\n  label: string;\n  children?: Option[];\n}\n\nconst options: Option[] = [\n  {\n    value: 'zhejiang',\n    label: 'Zhejiang',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'hangzhou',\n        label: 'Hangzhou',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'xihu',\n            label: 'West Lake',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'jiangsu',\n    label: 'Jiangsu',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'nanjing',\n        label: 'Nanjing',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'zhonghuamen',\n            label: 'Zhong Hua Men',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n];\n\nconst popupRender = (menus: React.ReactNode) => (\n  <div>\n    {menus}\n    <Divider style={{ margin: 0 }} />\n    <div style={{ padding: 8 }}>The footer is not very short.</div>\n  </div>\n);\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <Cascader options={options} popupRender={popupRender} placeholder=\"Please select\" />\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Placement\n\nYou can manually specify the position of the popup via `placement`.\n\n```tsx\nimport React, { useState } from 'react';\nimport type { RadioChangeEvent } from 'antd';\nimport { Cascader, Radio } from 'antd';\n\ninterface Option {\n  value: string;\n  label: string;\n  children?: Option[];\n}\n\nconst options: Option[] = [\n  {\n    value: 'zhejiang',\n    label: 'Zhejiang',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'hangzhou',\n        label: 'Hangzhou',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'xihu',\n            label: 'West Lake',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'jiangsu',\n    label: 'Jiangsu',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'nanjing',\n        label: 'Nanjing',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'zhonghuamen',\n            label: 'Zhong Hua Men',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n];\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => {\n  const [placement, setPlacement] = useState<'bottomLeft' | 'bottomRight' | 'topLeft' | 'topRight'>(\n    'topLeft',\n  );\n\n  const placementChange = (e: RadioChangeEvent) => {\n    setPlacement(e.target.value);\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <>\n      <Radio.Group value={placement} onChange={placementChange}>\n        <Radio.Button value=\"topLeft\">topLeft</Radio.Button>\n        <Radio.Button value=\"topRight\">topRight</Radio.Button>\n        <Radio.Button value=\"bottomLeft\">bottomLeft</Radio.Button>\n        <Radio.Button value=\"bottomRight\">bottomRight</Radio.Button>\n      </Radio.Group>\n      <br />\n      <br />\n      <Cascader options={options} placeholder=\"Please select\" placement={placement} />\n    </>\n  );\n};\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Variants\n\nVariants of Cascader, there are four variants: `outlined` `filled` `borderless` and `underlined`.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { Cascader, Flex } from 'antd';\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <Flex vertical gap=\"medium\">\n    <Cascader placeholder=\"Please select\" variant=\"borderless\" />\n    <Cascader placeholder=\"Please select\" variant=\"filled\" />\n    <Cascader placeholder=\"Please select\" variant=\"outlined\" />\n    <Cascader placeholder=\"Please select\" variant=\"underlined\" />\n  </Flex>\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Status\n\nAdd status to Cascader with `status`, which could be `error` or `warning`.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { Cascader, Space } from 'antd';\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => (\n  <Space vertical>\n    <Cascader status=\"error\" placeholder=\"Error\" />\n    <Cascader status=\"warning\" multiple placeholder=\"Warning multiple\" />\n  </Space>\n);\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### Custom semantic dom styling\n\nYou can customize the [semantic dom](#semantic-dom) style of Cascader by passing objects/functions through `classNames` and `styles`.\n\n```tsx\nimport React from 'react';\nimport { Cascader, Flex } from 'antd';\nimport type { CascaderProps, GetProp } from 'antd';\nimport { createStyles } from 'antd-style';\n\nconst useStyles = createStyles(({ token }) => {\n  return {\n    root: {\n      borderRadius: token.borderRadiusLG,\n    },\n  };\n});\n\ninterface Option {\n  value: string;\n  label: string;\n  children?: Option[];\n}\n\nconst options: Option[] = [\n  {\n    value: 'meet-student',\n    label: 'meet-student',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'hangzhou',\n        label: 'Hangzhou',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'xihu',\n            label: 'West Lake',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'jiangsu',\n    label: 'Jiangsu',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'nanjing',\n        label: 'Nanjing',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'zhonghuamen',\n            label: 'Zhong Hua Men',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n];\n\nconst stylesObject: CascaderProps['styles'] = {\n  prefix: {\n    color: '#ccc',\n  },\n  suffix: {\n    color: '#ccc',\n  },\n};\n\nconst stylesFn: CascaderProps['styles'] = (info): GetProp<CascaderProps, 'styles', 'Return'> => {\n  if (info.props.variant === 'filled') {\n    return {\n      prefix: {\n        color: '#1890ff',\n      },\n      suffix: {\n        color: '#1890ff',\n      },\n      popup: {\n        listItem: {\n          color: '#1890ff',\n        },\n      },\n    };\n  }\n  return {};\n};\n\nconst onChange: CascaderProps<Option>['onChange'] = (value) => {\n  console.log(value);\n};\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => {\n  const { styles: classNames } = useStyles();\n  return (\n    <Flex vertical gap=\"medium\">\n      <Cascader\n        options={options}\n        onChange={onChange}\n        placeholder=\"Object styles\"\n        classNames={classNames}\n        styles={stylesObject}\n        prefix=\"🏠\"\n      />\n      <Cascader\n        options={options}\n        onChange={onChange}\n        placeholder=\"Function  styles\"\n        variant=\"filled\"\n        classNames={classNames}\n        styles={stylesFn}\n        prefix=\"✅\"\n      />\n    </Flex>\n  );\n};\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n### = 5.10.0\">Panel\n\nUsed for inline view case.\n\n```tsx\nimport React, { useState } from 'react';\nimport type { CascaderProps } from 'antd';\nimport { Cascader, Flex, Switch } from 'antd';\n\ninterface Option {\n  value: string | number;\n  label: string;\n  children?: Option[];\n}\n\nconst options: Option[] = [\n  {\n    value: 'zhejiang',\n    label: 'Zhejiang',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'hangzhou',\n        label: 'Hangzhou',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'xihu',\n            label: 'West Lake',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n  {\n    value: 'jiangsu',\n    label: 'Jiangsu',\n    children: [\n      {\n        value: 'nanjing',\n        label: 'Nanjing',\n        children: [\n          {\n            value: 'zhonghuamen',\n            label: 'Zhong Hua Men',\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n];\n\nconst onChange: CascaderProps<Option>['onChange'] = (value) => {\n  console.log(value);\n};\n\nconst onMultipleChange: CascaderProps<Option, 'value', true>['onChange'] = (value) => {\n  console.log(value);\n};\n\nconst App: React.FC = () => {\n  const [disabled, setDisabled] = useState(false);\n\n  return (\n    <Flex vertical gap=\"small\" align=\"flex-start\">\n      <Switch\n        checked={disabled}\n        checkedChildren=\"Enabled\"\n        unCheckedChildren=\"Disabled\"\n        onChange={setDisabled}\n        aria-label=\"disabled switch\"\n      />\n      <Cascader.Panel options={options} onChange={onChange} disabled={disabled} />\n      <Cascader.Panel multiple options={options} onChange={onMultipleChange} disabled={disabled} />\n      <Cascader.Panel />\n    </Flex>\n  );\n};\n\nexport default App;\n```\n\n## API\n\nCommon props ref：[Common props](/docs/react/common-props)\n\n```jsx\n<Cascader options={options} onChange={onChange} />\n```\n\n| Property | Description | Type | Default | Version | [Global | 5.16.0 | × |\n\n### showSearch\n\n| Property | Description | Type | Default | Version |\n| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |\n| autoClearSearchValue | Whether the current search will be cleared on selecting an item. Option {\n  value: string | number;\n  label?: React.ReactNode;\n  disabled?: boolean;\n  children?: Option[];\n  // Determines if this is a leaf node(effective when `loadData` is specified).\n  // `false` will force trade TreeNode as a parent node.\n  // Show expand icon even if the current node has no children.\n  isLeaf?: boolean;\n}\n```\n\n## Methods\n\n| Name | Description | Version |\n| The main gains come from slimmer DatePicker and TimePicker runtime code in `@rc-component/picker`, plus Icon/Upload avoiding extra TwoTone runtime in the full bundle.
